    - heading "features / description:" [level=4]
    - text: "Upgrade your kitchen with the Frigidaire FRSS2623AS 25.6 Cu. Ft. side-by-side refrigerator. A standout feature for better food preservation is the advanced EvenTemp™ Cooling System, which quickly responds to temperature fluctuations to ensure a consistent, cold environment and significantly reduce freezer burn."
    - heading "EvenTemp™ Cooling System" [level=3]
    - text: "Prevents  warm spots, reduces  freezer burn, and maintains a  consistent temperature  throughout the fresh food and freezer compartments. This ensures optimal food preservation by quickly reacting to temperature fluctuations and constantly circulating cold air."
    - heading "PurePour™ Water and Ice Filter" [level=3]
    - text: "Keeps  safer, great-tasting water and ice  flowing by reducing up to 99% of contaminants. It also helps you  save money  and reduce plastic waste by cutting back on the cost of bottled water."
    - heading "High-Capacity Freezer Ice Maker" [level=3]
    - text: "Ensures you  always have plenty of ice on hand  for entertaining or daily use, as it holds 3.5 times more ice than the leading competitor."
    - heading "Fresh Storage Crispers" [level=3]
    - text: "Extends the life of your produce. These crispers feature a seal to block out dry air, creating an ideal, high-humidity environment to keep your  fruits and vegetables fresh for longer."
    - heading "External Water and Ice Dispenser" [level=3]
    - text: "Provides  convenient, instant access  to filtered water, crushed ice, and cube ice without needing to open the refrigerator door, which helps to conserve energy."
    - heading "Flexible Interior Organization" [level=3]
    - text: "Allows you to easily organize and  maximize storage space  for your family's favorite foods. The fresh food section includes three adjustable glass shelves and two adjustable gallon-sized door bins."
    - heading "Bright LED Lighting" [level=3]
    - text: "Provides  enhanced visibility  in both the fresh food and freezer sections, making it quick and easy to find items and reducing the time the door is left open."
    - heading "ENERGY STAR® Certified" [level=3]
    - text: "Saves money on utility bills  and maximizes energy efficiency because the appliance meets strict energy efficiency guidelines."
    - heading "Safety Alarms (Door Ajar and Power Failure)" [level=3]
    - text: "Offers  peace of mind  by alerting you if the door is accidentally left open or if the power has been interrupted, helping to prevent unnecessary food spoilage.\nWhy We Recommend This Model:\n\nA dependable side-by-side alternative when you want classic layout, clear organization, and external water/ice without paying premium prices.\nWell-suited for kitchens with a 36\" standard opening - makes replacements easier and avoids unexpected fit issues.\nENERGY STAR certified for efficient operation and lower utility costs while still offering ample 25.6 cu ft total capacity.\n\nBefore You Buy:\n\nThis is a standard-depth refrigerator - it will extend past cabinets unless you compare dimensions first.\nSide-by-side layouts typically have narrower shelves compared to French door models, which can matter if you often store wide platters or large items.\nA water line is required to use the external water and ice dispenser - without one, those features won’t function.\nThis model does not include smart/Wi-Fi features, so it’s best for buyers who want reliable basics rather than connected tech.\n\nApproximate Dimensions (Inches)Height: 69 7/8 Width: 36 1/8 Depth: 32 1/2 (without handles)Consult product specification sheet for exact dimensions."
